<UserId.>116937069908097571912</UserId.><username>Debrina Johnson</username><time>1463587769893</time><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Nice wine spot if you're passing thru Tehachapi or Mohave. I had a nice Cabernet Sauvignon.  You can get a half or full pour. Get the full pour it's a better value! They have a nice selection of wine many from California they also have a few international wines Chile, Italy, France. They also serve beer too, mostly artisan varieties. They have a pretty decent menu for food options salads, meat and cheese plates, pizza, and so much more. I had a flat bread pizza it was delicious. The salmon salad looked delicious! The chef used fresh ingredients! The don't allow children so leave the kiddos at home. They have nice bar seating or tables they even have a lounge area with comfy chairs and couches. This place is a little gem tucked in the middle of nowhere California.

Oh and you can take a bottle for the road if you like it.<//review>

< review>
Overall, this restaurant is a great place for lunch or dinner. The decor is modern with really warm colors. The only thing off-putting about this place is the mural over the bar... couldn't look away from the absurd garishness of that wall. The food was delicious but beware if you are on a date because everything is heavily cooked with garlic. We ordered flatbread with chimichurri sauce which was delicious but completely covered in garlic served with garlic oil. I ordered the chicken sandwich which had a delicate sliced chicken breast with tomatoes, lettuce, guacamole spread, and lots of garlic (raw and spread on the bread). My husband ordered the tri tip grilled cheese sandwich. It was yummy, gooey and buttery. Good thing we shared our sandwiches because the tri tip was so rich, it would be hard to eat a whole one! Lastly, my husband tried the icecream with port. It was more like a port float because there was so much port in the glass, it was overwhelming. By the end of the meal, my taste buds were destroyed from the heavy use of garlic and had bad breath the rest of the day. Service was good and there was even a live clarinet player to set the mood. We'll be back to try more items off the menu!< /review>

<user_name>Cindy Toh< /user_name>< rate>

< Text>
Cheap decent Chinese food.

Had a quick lunch stop over here before we headed for our short hike. There are metered parking lots along the road, fairly easy to get one during weekend lunch hour.

The shop is very dated and simple. One area which I dropped a star was due to the smell and ambience of this place. For the price I'm not expecting posh seats but it's never nice to walk in a restaurant that smells oily and musky. It the kind of place where you will walk out smelling like the restaurant.

We ordered a BBQ pork wanton soup and a beef Chow Fun. The BBQ pork wanton soup was disappointing, the wanton tasted bland and the pork tasted odd. The soup tasted alright.

The beef chow fun was good. The taste was great except that it's extremely oily. We continued eating but really felt guilty after gobbling them down.

The portions are fairly huge. They serve complimentary tea when you dine in the restaurant. For the two items we ordered, it was a total of $14!

For the price, you can't complain all that much.

Overall, a highly affordable decent Chinese food place.<//Text>

<UserId.>114897222954797640193< /UserId.>< user_name>
Kyle Young<//user_name>
<date>1525181978055< /date><rate>5< /rate>< text>
It's *absolutely* a five star as for a Cafe.

No fancy dish, no secret ingredient, almost nothing would get any food critic's attention; however, this is the place if you were looking for simple robust and solid Hong Kong style American Chinese food. The ingredients are simple, serving and service are robust, and the Hong Kong street vendor taste is solid - with the signature Wok texture/taste.

< Review>
I have been going here for twenty five years .You could spend 20 times more money and not get as good as the food here. Anyone who knows how to order at a Chinese restaurant knows you order your food not from a menu but from the wall. On the walls are pieces of paper that briefly describe a dish Let's say Rock Cod fillet with black bean .if you don't want black bean you order Rock Cod fillet with ginger and green onions. If you are at a loss for words you ask the only waiter at Suily's what you could get instead of black bean with your Rock Cod .your fillet will not have  inches of breading on it just fillet and your choice of sauce. Their fried flounder the best I've ever had.. they have gai lan  pork and beef  all cooked to your order in a wok five feet from your table at a half open kitchen .it's a small place but I'd rather go there than any other place in San Francisco. There is no decor other than clean simple and I only have eyes for the food.<//Review>

< text>
Mom and I went twice already. We ordered green enchiladas. The next time, we ordered bean and cheese burritos. So far, this is the best Mexican restaurant we eaten at that is not too far from home. Mom wishes their burritos had white cheese, but I think cheddar is more for the typical American palette. It added flavor to the burrito. The burrito was bigggggg!  I definitely give the burrito a solid 9. The enchiladas' green sauce was tasty and the taste did not over power the tortilla  or chicken. Service is fast and efficent.< /text>

Perhaps that's why I was brought a VERY  undercooked THIN CRUST pizza, when I ordered ORIGINAL CRUST.

A few weeks ago we ordered for delivery and got thin crust as well.
The thin crust SUCKS! I never order it, yet I've received it twice now.
I'm not the type to make the delivery driver stand there while I check my pizza, because I think it's rude to the driver. But if I do decide to give them a 3rd chance, I'm definitely making the driver wait while I double check the order.

Seriously, after the tip, I ended up spending $20 on ONE pizza that nobody wanted to eat because that thin crust tastes like greasy cardboard.

The whole reason I brag about Me N Ed's is the crust. And the last two pizzas I ordered had the worst crust ever. Especially that 2nd undercooked thin crust. So gross.

UPDATE
2/24/2019

Well, thanks to this specific manager, I will NOT be returning, and neither will anyone in my extended family. And that's a LOT OF CUSTOMERS YOU JUST LOST WITH YOUR APATHETIC, IMMATURE EXCUSES!

Kingsburg Me N Ed's is still the one to live up to. Selma's location can't even get close to the quality and customer service I get at the Kingsburg location. Kingsburg Me N Ed's gets 5 stars. Great food! Me N Eds is always delicious. For this location specifically in Selma, it does get packed at times which is understandable because the food is delicious.
